msg:This is a five-star hotel among five-star hotels. My husband and I went on a self-driving tour to Jiangshan City, Quzhou. We stayed for four nights. Every day, there were fruit snacks and small gifts delivered to the room, nail clipper sets, mobile phone holders, honey, etc. We were also upgraded to an executive river view king room for free. It was very comfortable. Both the front desk and the room staff would greet the guests warmly. There were four bottles of Nongfu Spring in the room every day, and several bottles of water were placed on the table near the elevator for guests who needed them to take. There was also laundry detergent in the room, which is not common in five-star hotels. I like the open large bathtub in the room the most. You can soak in the bathtub and watch the 60-inch LCD TV. It's very enjoyable. The hotel's underground garage is large and there are plenty of parking spaces. The hotel is 36 kilometers away from Jianglang Mountain, 63 kilometers away from Erbadu Ancient Town, 55 kilometers away from Tianji Longmen, 52 kilometers away from Xianxiaguan, and 73 kilometers away from Fugai Mountain. Jiangshan is so beautiful. I will definitely stay at this Jinling Hotel next time I come!
